# part A
# ive included the whole program
# so u can see what and why me do
.global _start
.data
        arr: .word 1, 2, 3, 4, 5

.text
_start:
        la x10, arr
        li x11, 20
        
        li x12, 0 
        loop:
                lw t0, 0(x10)
                add x12, x12, t0
                addi x10, x10, 4
                addi x11, x11, -4
                bgtz x11, loop ^LxXve9Rc
